<script type="text/javascript">

    function startApp() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            App.start();

            $('#logo').on('click', function() {
                var url = $(this).attr('href');
                App.tracking.trackEvent('home', 'Logo_Partner_Header', url);
            });

            $('.ss-footer .js-powered-by').on('click', function() {
                var url = $(this).attr('href');
                App.tracking.trackEvent('home', 'Logo_Footer', url);
            });
        });
    }


    /*
        &lt;text&gt; nodes are a wierd c# razor syntax for injecting javascript server-side
    */
        
        startApp();
        

</script>

    &lt;% } else { %&gt;

        &lt;div class="booking-dialog popup"&gt;
            &lt;a href="#" class="btn-close js-dialog-close"&gt;&lt;i class="ss-icon-close ss-icon"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
            &lt;div class="message"&gt;

                    &lt;%- messageHeader %&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
                &lt;div class="content"&gt;
                    &lt;%- messageContent %&gt;
                &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;% if(hasProgress) { %&gt;
            &lt;div class="js-dialog-progress"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;% } %&gt;
            &lt;div class="buttons-box &lt;% if(showClose &amp;&amp; continueLink){ print('two-buttons')} %&gt;"&gt;
                &lt;% if(showClose) { %&gt;
                &lt;button class="js-dialog-close btn-gray" data-i18n="common.close"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;
                &lt;% } %&gt;
                &lt;% if(continueLink) { %&gt;
                &lt;button class="js-dialog-continue btn-cyan &lt;% showClose ? print('') : print('fill') %&gt;" data-i18n="common.continue"&gt;&lt;/button&gt;

            &lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;

    &lt;% } %&gt;
